In the case of Joe Biden's credit card, let's assume it follows the standard structure of a Visa credit card. The first digit, also known as the major industry identifier (MII), would be 4, indicating that it's a Visa card. The next 15 digits are divided into four groups: the issuer identification number (IIN), the account number, the check digit, and the verification value.

The IIN, which consists of the first six digits, is unique to each issuer and is used to identify the credit card company that issued the card. The account number, which makes up the next nine digits, is unique to the individual account holder and is used to identify the specific card. The check digit, which is the 15th digit, is used to verify the integrity of the credit card
